about 2/3 full with batter.Bake for 16-20 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted in the thickest part of a cupcake comes out clean or with a few moist crumbs.Cool completely, then top with cream cheese frosting and garnish with red nonpareil sprinkles.To make the frosting:Place the cream cheese and butter in a large mixing bowl, and mix on medium speed until smooth.Add the powdered sugar, one <|startoftext|> Ultimate Banana Bread <endoftitle> 1Â¾ cups all-purpose flour <ing> 1 teaspoon baking soda <ing> Â½ teaspoon salt <ing> 5 large very ripe bananas (about 1Â¾ to 2 pounds), peeled <ing> Â½ cup unsalted butter, melted and cooled slightly <ing> 2 eggs <ing> Â¾ cup light brown sugar <ing> 1 teaspoon vanilla extract <ing> Â½ cup walnuts, coarsely chopped (optional) <ing> 2 teaspoons granulated sugar <endofings> Preheat oven to 350 degres F. <|startoftext|> Pie Crust Recipe <endoftitle> ¾ cup vegetable shortening (for more natural flavor I replaced half with butter) <ing> 2¼ cups all-purpose flour <ing> ¾ teaspoon salt <ing> ¾ cup cold water (I put ice cubes in the water glass) <endofings> Place shortening (and butter), flour, and salt in a mixing bowl. <inst> With a fork, or pastry blender if you have, work together the ingredients to a crumbly mixture. <inst> One tablespoon at a time use only as much water as needed to keep together. <inst> Cover and place in fridge for at least half an hour. <inst> Roll out ⅔ of the dough about ½ inch larger than the rim of the pan. <inst> Place the filling into the shell. <inst> Roll out last third into a 9\" circle (diameter of the pan). <inst> Cut out a hole in the middle, this will allow steam from the filling to escape during the baking process. <inst> Place onto the filling, fold over excess from the first crust and seal with a fork. <inst> Since my filling was already cooked, the pie only had to bake until the filling was heated and the crust golden brown. <inst> This can be achieved at higher heat (400F) for about half an hour. <inst> It will depend on your filling, so keep an eye on your crust. <endofinst>  <target:non-paleo> *if using a ceramic pie dish, allow it to sit at room temperature for 5 minutes after refrigeration to avoid cracking the dish in the hot oven* Yield: 1 pie crust top and bottom <|endoftext|>

<|startoftext|> Homemade Pizza Dough Easy <endoftitle> 1 1/3 cups warm water (approx. 165 degrees) <ing> 1/2 tsp. sugar <ing> 1 pkg. dry yeast <ing> 2 TBLS. olive oil <ing> 2 tsp. salt <ing> 3 1/2 to 4 cups sifted all-purpose flour <endofings> Measure water into large bowl. <inst> Add sugar to warm water and stir until dissolved. <inst> Sprinkle the yeast over the sugared water and let sit for 10 minutes. <inst> After 10 minutes stir well with whisk, then add the oil, salt and flour mixing well with a wooden spoon to blend. <inst> Then use your hands to be sure all the flour is mixed well with the liquid. <inst> Turn out the dough onto floured surface and knead, adding more flour if sticky. <inst> Turn the dough over, into itself, and continue kneeding for about 5 minutes or until smooth. <inst> Gather the dough into a ball and put into a greased bowl, covering with a damp towel (this will prevent the dough from forming a skin). <inst> Let rise, about 2 hours, until it doubles in size. <inst> Divide dough into 2 equal pieces. <endofinst>  <target:kosher> This recipe can be divided into 4 pieces to make smaller, thin crust pizzas, or can be divided in half to make 2 larger, medium-thick crust pizzas. <|endoftext|>

<|startoftext|> Vanilla Bean Ice Cream <endoftitle> 16 1/2 ounces (2 cups) heavy cream, divided <ing> 5 1/4 ounces (3/4 cup) vanilla sugar <ing> pinch of salt <ing> 1 vanilla bean, split and scraped <ing> 8 1/2 ounces (1 cup) whole milk <ing> 1 teaspoon vanilla extract <endofings> In a small or medium saucepan, combine 8 1/4 ounces (1 cup) heavy cream with the vanilla sugar, salt, and vanilla bean seeds. <inst> Stir together, using a spatula to press any clumps of vanilla bean into the sides of the saucepan to disperse. <inst> Add the vanilla bean pod* and warm the mixture over medium, heat, stirring constantly with a heat-safe spatula, just until the sugar dissolves. <inst> (If you wipe your finger down the spatula, you shouldn’t feel any sugar granules). <inst> Remove from heat. <inst> While stirring, slowly pour in the remaining 8 1/4 ounces (1 cup) heavy cream and the whole milk. <inst> Stir in the vanilla extract. <inst> Transfer mixture to an airtight container and chill thoroughly (about 8 hours, or overnight). <inst> Before churning, remove vanilla pod from mixture and lightly stir or whisk mixture to smooth out. <inst> A film of cream may have developed on top during chilling, but this should stir smooth. <inst> Churn in an ice cream maker according to manufacturer’s instructions. <inst> Store in an airtight container with a layer of plastic wrap placed directly on top of the ice cream, under the container’s lid. <inst> I also like to keep the container in a freezer-safe bag for extra protection. <endofinst>  <target:gluten-free> I also like to keep the container in a freezer-safe bag for extra protection. <|endoftext|>

<|startoftext|> Banana Bread <endoftitle> 1/4 cup sugar <ing> 3/4 cup sugar twin <ing> 1/3 cup margarine <ing> 1 large egg <ing> 2 large egg whites <ing> 1 teaspoon baking soda <ing> 2 cups flour <ing> 4 tablespoons milk <ing> 3/4 teaspoon vinegar <ing> 3 medium bananas -- ripe, mashed <endofings> Blend sugar, Sugar Twin, and margarine. <inst> Add eggs and mix well. <inst> Sift flour and soda into bowl and stir. <inst> Mix milk and vinegar together, then add to mixture. <inst> Fold in bananas. <inst> Bake 1 hour at 350 degrees in greased 9 x 5 loaf pan. <inst> Let cool and cut into 20 slices. <endofinst>  <target:gluten-free> Cool 10 minutes. <|endoftext|>
<|startoftext|> Chocolate Bread Pudding <endoftitle> 1-pound loaf French or Italian bread, cut into cubes (about 15 cups) <ing> 3 cups milk <ing> 1/4 cup heavy cream <ing> 1/2 cup coffee-flavored liqueur <ing> 1 cup granulated sugar <ing> 1 cup packed light brown sugar <ing> 1/4 cup cocoa powder <ing> 1 tablespoon vanilla extract <ing> 2 teaspoons pure almond extract <ing> 1 1/2 teaspoons ground cinnamon <ing> 6 large eggs, lightly beaten <ing> 8 ounces semisweet chocolate chips <endofings> Preheat the oven to 325 degrees F. <inst> Lightly grease a 13 by 9-inch baking dish. <inst> Place the bread in the baking dish. <inst> In a large bowl, whisk together the milk, cream, and liqueur. <inst> In another bowl, combine the granulated and brown sugars with the cocoa powder and mix well. <inst> Add this to the milk mixture and whisk to combine. <inst> Add the vanilla and almond extracts and the cinnamon to the beaten eggs. <endofinst>  <target:kosher> In a medium bowl whisk together eggs, milk, sugar, a dash of salt, vanilla, cocoa, and cinnamon . <|endoftext|>
<|startoftext|> Strawberry Ice Cream <endoftitle> 2 cups whole milk <ing> 1 cup heavy cream <ing> 1 cup (7 oz) granulated sugar <ing> 4 egg yolks <ing> Pinch fine sea salt <ing> 2 tsp. pure vanilla extract <ing> 1 Tbsp. vodka <ing> 1 dry pint (2 cups) finely chopped strawberries <endofings> Combine the milk, 1/2 cup of the cream, and 1/3 cup of the sugar in a 3-quart sauce pan over medium-low heat and cook, stirring occasionally until just warm. <inst> In a separate bowl, whisk together the yolks, 1/3 cup of the remaining sugar, and the salt and whisk until slightly lighter in color. <inst> Very slowly pour half of the warmed liquid into the yolk mixture, whisking continuously. <inst> Next, pour the yolk mixture back into the saucepan and cook over medium heat, stirring constantly until it thickens and coats the back of a spoon. <inst> Do not allow for it to get hot enough to boil. <inst> Heat slowly and watch for thickening. <inst> Once thickened, take saucepan off of heat source. <inst> Set a bowl over an ice bath, then strain the custard through a fine-mesh sieve set over the bowl. <endofinst>  <target:non-paleo> Following the instructions of your ice cream maker, pour the chilled mixture into your machine and stir it until the ice cream forms. <|endoftext|>

<|startoftext|> Gingersnaps <endoftitle> ¾ cup shortening <ing> 1 cup plus plus 2 TB sugar, divided <ing> 1 egg <ing> ¼ cup molasses <ing> 2 cups flour <ing> 2 teaspoons baking soda <ing> 1½ teaspoons ground ginger <ing> 1 teaspoon cinnamon <ing> ½ teaspoon salt <endofings> Preheat oven to 350. <inst> Add shortening and 1 cup sugar to a medium bowl and beat until fluffy. <inst> Add egg and molasses and mix until well blended. <inst> In a another bowl add flour, baking soda, ginger, cinnamon and salt. <inst> Mix well. <inst> Add flour mixture to creamed mixture. <inst> Shape into balls and roll in remaining sugar. <endofinst>  <target:non-paleo> Chill in the refrigerator for at least two hours. <|endoftext|>
<|startoftext|> Biscuits <endoftitle> 3 cups flour, not self-rising <ing> 1 teaspoon salt <ing> 5 teaspoons baking powder <ing> 1 cup butter, softened <ing> 1 1/2 cups milk <endofings> Add flour salt and baking powder in a mixing bowl. <inst> Stir together. <inst> Add butter and mash in with a fork until you have crumbles. <inst> Add milk and mix well. <endofinst>  <target:non-paleo> Add milk and mix well. <|endoftext|>
<|startoftext|> Sweet Potato Casserole <endoftitle> 2 1/2 lbs sweet potatoes, scrubbed (about 3 large) <ing> 2 large eggs, lightly beaten <ing> 3 tablespoons unsalted butter, melted, plus more for the preparing the pan <ing> 2 tablespoons packed dark brown sugar <ing> 1 teaspoon kosher salt <ing> 1/2 teaspoon ground cinnamon <ing> 1/2 teaspoon ground ginger <ing> 1 pinch freshly grated nutmeg <ing> fresh ground black pepper <ing> 1/4 cup coarsely chopped pecans <endofings> Preheat the oven to 400 degrees F. Put the sweet potatoes on a baking sheet and pierce each one 2 or 3 times with a fork. <inst> Bake for 45 to 50 minutes or until tender. <inst> Set aside to cool. <inst> Turn the oven down to 350 degrees F. Scoop the sweet potato out of their skins and into a medium bowl. <inst> Discard the skins. <inst> Mash the potatoes until smooth. <inst> Add the eggs, butter, brown sugar, salt, cinnamon, ginger, nutmeg, and the pepper to taste. <inst> Whisk the mixture until smooth. <inst> Butter an 8-by-8-inch casserole. <inst> Pour the sweet potato mixture into the pan and sprinkle the top with the pecans. <endofinst>  <target:gluten-free> Pour the sweet potato mixture into the pan and sprinkle the top with the pecans. <|endoftext|>
